var host_server='https://scan.coverity.com';

function checkNomination(){
	project_name=$("#projects-hierarchies-nav .selected").text();
        project_id=$("#projectId").val();
	cid_selected=$("#table-details-grid .cid.selected").text();
	if(cid_selected == ""){
	       return;
	}
        user_name='simtiaz@ncsu.edu';
	url_check=host_server + "/defect_nominations/check?cid=" + cid_selected + "&project_name=" + project_name + "&user="+ user_name;
        $.ajax({
            type: "GET",
            url: url_check,
            success:  function(msg,status){
		if(msg.status == 'nominated' && cid_selected == $("#table-details-grid .cid.selected").text()){
			$("#source-browser-defect-nominate").text(" Already nominated ")
		}
		else if ($("#source-browser-defect-nominate").text() == "Already nominated"){
			$("#source-browser-defect-nominate").text(" Nominate Defect ")
		} 
	    } 
        });

}

function nominateDefect(cid_selected){
	project_name=$("#projects-hierarchies-nav .selected").text();
	project_id=$("#projectId").val();
	if(cid_selected == ""){
		cid_selected=$("#table-details-grid .cid.selected").text()
	}
	user_name=$("#user-name-container-id").text()
	url_new=host_server + "/defect_nominations/new?cid=" + cid_selected + "&project_name=" + project_name ; 
	$.popupWindow(url_new, {
              width: 1000,
              height: 800,
              center: 'screen',
	      createNew: false,
	      location: true,
	      toolbar: true,
	      scrollbars: true
          });
}
function inIframe() {
    try {
        return window.self !== window.top;
    } catch (e) {
        return true;
    }
}

function runDemoFromMenu()
{
  runDemo();
}

function showViews(){
  if( $("#sections-nav").attr("class") != "open")
	$("#views-button").click(); 
}

function showViewsAndNext(){
  showViews(); 
  setTimeout(guiders.next,1000);
}

function hideViews(){
  if( $("#sections-nav").attr("class") == "open")
	$("#views-button").click();
}

function runDemo()
{
    guiders.createGuider({
      closeOnEscape: true,
      buttons: [{name: "Yes, let's go",classString: "primary-button", onclick: guiders.next}, {name: "No thanks.",onclick: guiders.hideAll, classString: "non-primary-button"   }],
      xButton: true,
      description: "<br>Here's a quick guided tour about Coverity Scan User Interface! Would you like to begin?",
      id: "first",
      next: "1.5",
      overlay: true,
      title: "Welcome to Coverity Scan Guided Tour!"
    }).show();


   guiders.createGuider({
      closeOnEscape: true,
      attachTo: "#views-button",
      buttons: [ {name: "Back"}, {name: "Next"}],
      xButton: true,
description: "<br>Click to toggle the list of views. ",
      id: "1.5",
      next: "second",
      position: 3,
      onShow: showViews,
      offset: { left: 0, top: 5 },
      width: 200,
      title: "View pane"
    });

    guiders.createGuider({
      closeOnEscape: true,
      attachTo: "#table-view-views",
      buttons: [ {name: "Back"}, {name: "Next"}],
      xButton: true,

function isDefectLoaded(){
      try{
        if( $(".ui-widget-content.slick-row.even").children().size() > 0)
              return true;  
      }
      catch(err){
      }
      return false;
}

  window.onload = function() {
    if(inIframe())
	return;
    if (jQuery.cookie('COV_SCAN_NO_SHOW_WIZ')) {
      return;
    } else {
      var intervalId = setInterval( function() {
          if(isDefectLoaded()){
		clearInterval(intervalId);
		jQuery.cookie('COV_SCAN_NO_SHOW_WIZ', true, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
                runDemo();
	 } 
      }, 500);
    }
  }

var host_server='https://scan.coverity.com';

function checkNomination(){
	project_name=$("#projects-hierarchies-nav .selected").text();
        project_id=$("#projectId").val();
	cid_selected=$("#table-details-grid .cid.selected").text();
	if(cid_selected == ""){
	       return;
	}
        user_name='simtiaz@ncsu.edu';
	url_check=host_server + "/defect_nominations/check?cid=" + cid_selected + "&project_name=" + project_name + "&user="+ user_name;
        $.ajax({
            type: "GET",
            url: url_check,
            success:  function(msg,status){
		if(msg.status == 'nominated' && cid_selected == $("#table-details-grid .cid.selected").text()){
			$("#source-browser-defect-nominate").text(" Already nominated ")
		}
		else if ($("#source-browser-defect-nominate").text() == "Already nominated"){
			$("#source-browser-defect-nominate").text(" Nominate Defect ")
		} 
	    } 
        });

}

function nominateDefect(cid_selected){
	project_name=$("#projects-hierarchies-nav .selected").text();
	project_id=$("#projectId").val();
	if(cid_selected == ""){
		cid_selected=$("#table-details-grid .cid.selected").text()
	}
	user_name=$("#user-name-container-id").text()
	url_new=host_server + "/defect_nominations/new?cid=" + cid_selected + "&project_name=" + project_name ; 
	$.popupWindow(url_new, {
              width: 1000,
              height: 800,
              center: 'screen',
	      createNew: false,
	      location: true,
	      toolbar: true,
	      scrollbars: true
          });
}
function inIframe() {
    try {
        return window.self !== window.top;
    } catch (e) {
        return true;
    }
}

{
  runDemo();
}

  if( $("#sections-nav").attr("class") != "open")
	$("#views-button").click();

  showViews(); 
  setTimeout(guiders.next,1000);
}

  if( $("#sections-nav").attr("class") == "open")
	$("#views-button").click();
}

function isDefectLoaded(){
      try{
        if( $(".ui-widget-content.slick-row.even").children().size() > 0)
              return true;  
      }
      catch(err){
      }
      return false;

	return;

	 } 
      }, 500);
    }

var host_server='https://scan.coverity.com';

function checkNomination(){
	project_name=$("#projects-hierarchies-nav .selected").text();
        project_id=$("#projectId").val();
	cid_selected=$("#table-details-grid .cid.selected").text();
	if(cid_selected == ""){
	       return;
	}
        user_name='simtiaz@ncsu.edu';
	url_check=host_server + "/defect_nominations/check?cid=" + cid_selected + "&project_name=" + project_name + "&user="+ user_name;
        $.ajax({
            type: "GET",
            url: url_check,
            success:  function(msg,status){
		if(msg.status == 'nominated' && cid_selected == $("#table-details-grid .cid.selected").text()){
			$("#source-browser-defect-nominate").text(" Already nominated ")
		}
		else if ($("#source-browser-defect-nominate").text() == "Already nominated"){
			$("#source-browser-defect-nominate").text(" Nominate Defect ")
		} 
	    } 
        });

}

function nominateDefect(cid_selected){
	project_name=$("#projects-hierarchies-nav .selected").text();
	project_id=$("#projectId").val();
	if(cid_selected == ""){
		cid_selected=$("#table-details-grid .cid.selected").text()
	}
	user_name=$("#user-name-container-id").text()
	url_new=host_server + "/defect_nominations/new?cid=" + cid_selected + "&project_name=" + project_name ; 
	$.popupWindow(url_new, {
              width: 1000,
              height: 800,
              center: 'screen',
	      createNew: false,
	      location: true,
	      toolbar: true,
	      scrollbars: true
          });
}
function inIframe() {
    try {
        return window.self !== window.top;
    } catch (e) {
        return true;
    }
}

{
  runDemo();
}

  if( $("#sections-nav").attr("class") != "open")
	$("#views-button").click(); 
}

  showViews(); 
  setTimeout(guiders.next,1000);
}

function hideViews(){
  if( $("#sections-nav").attr("class") == "open")
	$("#views-button").click();
}

function isDefectLoaded(){
      try{
        if( $(".ui-widget-content.slick-row.even").children().size() > 0)
              return true;  
      }
      catch(err){
      }
      return false;
}

    if(inIframe())
	return;

      return;

                runDemo();
	 } 
      }, 500);
    }

var host_server='https://scan.coverity.com';

function checkNomination(){
	project_name=$("#projects-hierarchies-nav .selected").text();
        project_id=$("#projectId").val();
	cid_selected=$("#table-details-grid .cid.selected").text();
	if(cid_selected == ""){
	       return;
	}
        user_name='simtiaz@ncsu.edu';
	url_check=host_server + "/defect_nominations/check?cid=" + cid_selected + "&project_name=" + project_name + "&user="+ user_name;
        $.ajax({
            type: "GET",
            url: url_check,
            success:  function(msg,status){
		if(msg.status == 'nominated' && cid_selected == $("#table-details-grid .cid.selected").text()){
			$("#source-browser-defect-nominate").text(" Already nominated ")
		}
		else if ($("#source-browser-defect-nominate").text() == "Already nominated"){
			$("#source-browser-defect-nominate").text(" Nominate Defect ")
		} 
	    } 
        });

}

function nominateDefect(cid_selected){
	project_name=$("#projects-hierarchies-nav .selected").text();
	project_id=$("#projectId").val();
	if(cid_selected == ""){
		cid_selected=$("#table-details-grid .cid.selected").text()
	}
	user_name=$("#user-name-container-id").text()
	url_new=host_server + "/defect_nominations/new?cid=" + cid_selected + "&project_name=" + project_name ; 
	$.popupWindow(url_new, {
              width: 1000,
              height: 800,
              center: 'screen',
	      createNew: false,
	      location: true,
	      toolbar: true,
	      scrollbars: true
          });
}
function inIframe() {
    try {
        return window.self !== window.top;
    } catch (e) {
        return true;
    }
}

function runDemoFromMenu()
{
  runDemo();
}

function showViews(){
  if( $("#sections-nav").attr("class") != "open")
	$("#views-button").click(); 
}

function showViewsAndNext(){
  showViews(); 
  setTimeout(guiders.next,1000);
}

function hideViews(){
  if( $("#sections-nav").attr("class") == "open")
	$("#views-button").click();
}

function runDemo()
{
    guiders.createGuider({
      closeOnEscape: true,
      buttons: [{name: "Yes, let's go",classString: "primary-button", onclick: guiders.next}, {name: "No thanks.",onclick: guiders.hideAll, classString: "non-primary-button"   }],
      xButton: true,
      description: "<br>Here's a quick guided tour about Coverity Scan User Interface! Would you like to begin?",
      id: "first",
      next: "1.5",
      overlay: true,
      title: "Welcome to Coverity Scan Guided Tour!"
    }).show();


   guiders.createGuider({
      closeOnEscape: true,
      attachTo: "#views-button",
      buttons: [ {name: "Back"}, {name: "Next"}],
      xButton: true,
description: "<br>Click to toggle the list of views. ",
      id: "1.5",
      next: "second",
      position: 3,
      onShow: showViews,
      offset: { left: 0, top: 5 },
      width: 200,
      title: "View pane"
    });

    guiders.createGuider({
      closeOnEscape: true,
      attachTo: "#table-view-views",
      buttons: [ {name: "Back"}, {name: "Next"}],
      xButton: true,
description: "<br>The most common view is 'Outstanding Defects', in this view you will see all existing defects from the LAST build submitted. Other views just filter these defects by high impact or other ways. <br/><br/>Click on <b>'Outstanding Defects'</b> view",
      id: "second",
      next: "three",
      position: 2,
      onShow: showViews,
      offset: { left: 0, top: 100 },
      title: "View pane"
    });


    guiders.createGuider({
      closeOnEscape: true,
      attachTo: "#table-details-grid",
      buttons: [ {name: "Back"}, {name: "Next"}],
      xButton: true,
description: "<br>This view shows all the defects based on the filters defined the view. <br/> <br/>Click on one of the defects to view the details.",
      id: "three",
      next: "ten",
      position: 6,
      onShow: hideViews,
      offset: { left: -100, top: -100 },
      title: "Defect pane"
    });

    guiders.createGuider({
      closeOnEscape: true,
      buttons: [{name: "OK",classString: "primary-button", onclick: function a(){guiders.hideAll();guiders.show("three")} }],
      description: "<br>Click on the first defect (CID).<br>If you don't see the defect, make sure to select 'Outstanding Defects' view from the left pane.",
      id: "ten",
      next: "fourth",
      shouldSkip: function triageVisible(){if (!TableView.triageDetailsView.model.attributes.mergedDefectCID) {return false;} else  { return true;}},
      title: "Select Defect"
    });

    guiders.createGuider({
      closeOnEscape: true,
      attachTo: "#table-view-source",
      buttons: [  {name: "Back"}, {name: "Next"}],
      xButton: true,
      description: "<br>The sophisticated source browser helps you understand the issue. Red and green numbered messages identify the code path, including relevant variables, code browsing and folding. Clicking on symbols in your code allow you to navigate like a pro! <br/><br/> Click on Next to proceed.",
     id: "fourth",
      next: "seventh",
      position: 2,
      title: "Source pane",
width: 200
    });

function isDefectLoaded(){
      try{
        if( $(".ui-widget-content.slick-row.even").children().size() > 0)
              return true;  
      }
      catch(err){
      }
      return false;
}

  window.onload = function() {
    if(inIframe())
	return;
    if (jQuery.cookie('COV_SCAN_NO_SHOW_WIZ')) {
      return;
    } else {
      var intervalId = setInterval( function() {
          if(isDefectLoaded()){
		clearInterval(intervalId);
		jQuery.cookie('COV_SCAN_NO_SHOW_WIZ', true, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
                runDemo();
	 } 
      }, 500);
    }
  }

var host_server='https://scan.coverity.com';

function checkNomination(){
	project_name=$("#projects-hierarchies-nav .selected").text();
        project_id=$("#projectId").val();
	cid_selected=$("#table-details-grid .cid.selected").text();
	if(cid_selected == ""){
	       return;
	}
        user_name='simtiaz@ncsu.edu';
	url_check=host_server + "/defect_nominations/check?cid=" + cid_selected + "&project_name=" + project_name + "&user="+ user_name;
        $.ajax({
            type: "GET",
            url: url_check,
            success:  function(msg,status){
		if(msg.status == 'nominated' && cid_selected == $("#table-details-grid .cid.selected").text()){
			$("#source-browser-defect-nominate").text(" Already nominated ")
		}
		else if ($("#source-browser-defect-nominate").text() == "Already nominated"){
			$("#source-browser-defect-nominate").text(" Nominate Defect ")
		} 
	    } 
        });

}

function nominateDefect(cid_selected){
	project_name=$("#projects-hierarchies-nav .selected").text();
	project_id=$("#projectId").val();
	if(cid_selected == ""){
		cid_selected=$("#table-details-grid .cid.selected").text()
	}
	user_name=$("#user-name-container-id").text()
	url_new=host_server + "/defect_nominations/new?cid=" + cid_selected + "&project_name=" + project_name ; 
	$.popupWindow(url_new, {
              width: 1000,
              height: 800,
              center: 'screen',
	      createNew: false,
	      location: true,
	      toolbar: true,
	      scrollbars: true
          });
}
function inIframe() {
    try {
        return window.self !== window.top;
    } catch (e) {
        return true;
    }
}

function runDemoFromMenu()
{
  runDemo();
}

function showViews(){
  if( $("#sections-nav").attr("class") != "open")
	$("#views-button").click(); 
}

function showViewsAndNext(){
  showViews(); 
  setTimeout(guiders.next,1000);
}

function hideViews(){
  if( $("#sections-nav").attr("class") == "open")
	$("#views-button").click();
}

function runDemo()
{
    guiders.createGuider({
      closeOnEscape: true,

      description: "<br>Here's a quick guided tour about Coverity Scan User Interface! Would you like to begin?",

      next: "1.5",
      overlay: true,
      title: "Welcome to Coverity Scan Guided Tour!"
    }).show();


   guiders.createGuider({

      attachTo: "#views-button",
      buttons: [ {name: "Back"}, {name: "Next"}],
      xButton: true,
description: "<br>Click to toggle the list of views. ",

    });

      id: "second",
      next: "three",
      position: 2,
      onShow: showViews,

      xButton: true,
      buttons: [  {name: "Back"}, {name: "Next"}],
      description: "<br>What if I have many defects? Where do I start? <br/>We recommend 'Outstanding defects by category' view; choose the ones you care about. You could also create your own filter and view. <br/><br/>Mouse over on 'Outstanding defects' view and click on pull-down menu icon. Once the pull-down menu appears, click on 'Edit settings...', and you can modify the filters or add columns.  ",
      id: "eighth",
      next: "nineth",
      position: 2,
      offset: { left: 0, top: 0 },
      onShow: showViews,
      title: "Getting Started",
      width: 400
    });

    guiders.createGuider({
      closeOnEscape: true,
      buttons: [  {name: "Back"}, {name: "Close" , onclick:  function b(){guiders.hideAll();hideViews() } }],
      description: "<br>Now that you've had a quick tour, feel free to browse around the project's defects!",
     id: "nineth",
      onClose: hideViews(),
      onHide: hideViews(),
      title: "Let's get started!"
    });


}

function isDefectLoaded(){
      try{
        if( $(".ui-widget-content.slick-row.even").children().size() > 0)
              return true;  
      }
      catch(err){
      }
      return false;
}

  window.onload = function() {
    if(inIframe())
	return;
    if (jQuery.cookie('COV_SCAN_NO_SHOW_WIZ')) {
      return;
    } else {
      var intervalId = setInterval( function() {
          if(isDefectLoaded()){
		clearInterval(intervalId);
		jQuery.cookie('COV_SCAN_NO_SHOW_WIZ', true, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
                runDemo();
	 } 
      }, 500);
    }
  }
